Shipping Information

   Depending on security we ship from either: Germany Holland or Belgium.
   As of 2 april we are shipping from Germany.
   NON-TRACKED
   Single or combined orders under 500 euro:
   We ship worldwide except for the U.S.A , Israel, Australia and the
   Netherlands.
   1. Products are first weighed, double checked, and then vacuumed.
   2. Next products are heat sealed into an odor free aluminum bag.
   We use business like envelopes with printed labels and ship out your
   order within 24-48 hours after we have received full payment in
   bitcoin. Weekends not included.
   Multiple orders are automatically combined and sent in one package.
   TRACKED:
   Single orders or combined orders of 500 euros or more.
   If you have multiple orders of more than 500 euros please order our
   tracking listing to make sure your order is sent tracked.
   For security reasons we do not give tracking codes to customers, unless
   there is a problem with the post office or courier in your country.
   We can track your item for you if needed, 5 days after your order has
   been shipped.
   TRACKED ORDERS ARE SHIPPED AS PARCELS and have a success rate of
   99.8%!! The small 0.2% loss
   is mostly due to address mistakes, so double check your address!
   DELIVERY TIME AVERAGES:
   1-10 Days: Western and Northern Europe
   4-14 Days: East and Southern Europe and Canada
   10-60 Days: Australia, New-Zealand, Brazil, Russia, and Asia.
   These are average delivery times. After having shipped thousands and
   thousands of parcels
   worldwide we KNOW that delivery times cannot be accurately predicted,
   it's impossible.
   AVERAGE DELIVERY SUCCESS RATES:
   Germany: 99.9% Alle Deutsche Kunden sind Wilkommen!
   Austria: 90%
   France 85%
   United Kingdom 85%
   Italy: 90%
   EU-average: 98%
   World Average: 90%
   RESHIP POLICY:
   Please only contact us for a missing package after:
   1. German customers 7 days AFTER we have actually shipped.
   2. 14 days Western and Northern Europe
   3. 21 days Eastern and Southern Europe
   4. 28 days Rest of the world
   You are entitled to one 50% reship for every 4 successful orders that
   you have made with us.
   This reship cannot exceed the average weight of the 4 successful
   orders. All other orders you
   have had with us on past market places count as well.
   Tracked orders are rarely lost , if something goes wrong please contact
   us personally.
   ALWAYS CONTACT US if something does not arrive, we make refund
   decisions on a case by case basis
   and we are easy to get along with.
   We are here to help you out if something goes wrong. Thanks!!

Gold / Platinum Members

   GOLD MEMBER:
   Once you have ordered for 5.000 euros or more under the same account in
   this shop you will be awarded the status GOLD MEMBER.
   Our shop automatically keeps track of your status and for how many
   euros you have ordered.
   If you have ordered for more than 5.000 euros with us in the past
   please contact us with past usernames in past market places and we can
   upgrade your status to GOLD MEMBER.
   Gold Member listings are at a discount (cheaper) and are only valid if
   you have the gold member status.
   We only have limited gold member listings. Not everything can be
   listed.
   PLATINUM MEMBER:
   Platinum member status applies to accounts that have ordered for 50.000

   Official Description:
   Girl Scout Cookies, or GSC, is an OG Kush and Durban Poison hybrid
   cross whose reputation grew too large to stay within the borders of its
   California homeland. With a sweet and earthy aroma, Girl Scout Cookies
   launches you to euphoria’s top floor where full-body relaxation meets a
   time-bending cerebral space. A little goes a long way with this hybrid,
   whose THC heights have won Girl Scout Cookies numerous Cannabis Cup
   awards. Patients needing a strong dose of relief, however, may look to
   GSC for severe pain, nausea, and appetite loss.
   There are several different phenotypes of the Girl Scout Cookies strain
   including Thin Mint and Platinum Cookies, which exhibit some variation
   in appearance and effect. Typically, however, Girl Scout Cookies
   expresses its beauty in twisting green calyxes wrapped in purple leaves
   and fiery orange hairs. Patients and consumers looking to cultivate
   this cannabis staple themselves should wait 9 to 10 weeks for their
   indoor plants to finish flowering.

   The largest online coffee-shop in the world.

   [Product photo]

   FREE SHIPPING
   1. All orders need to payed in Bitcoin before we can ship your order.
   2. Postal delivery times vary, check our homepage for further
   information.
   3. We do NOT ship to the U.S.A , Israel or the Netherlands.
   Please check our homepage before mailing us. It's only five minutes of
   your time and it answers most questions.
   Official Product Description:
   Among the most famous strains worldwide is White Widow, a balanced
   hybrid first bred in the Netherlands by Green House Seeds. A cross
   between a Brazilian sativa landrace and a resin-heavy South Indian
   indica, White Widow has blessed every Dutch coffee shop menu since its
   birth in the 1990s. Its buds are white with crystal resin, warning you
   of the potent effects to come. A powerful burst of euphoria and energy
   breaks through immediately, stimulating both conversation and
   creativity. White Widow’s genetics have given rise to many other
   legends like White Russian, White Rhino, and Blue Widow. Still, many
   growers prefer cultivation of the original White Widow, which flowers
   in about 60 days indoors.
   Dutch Magic Description:
   This strain is what harvesters call white widow, its the most common
   sold weed in Holland so it has one of the best price/ratio for
   resellers. It is one of the best selling products we have.

   from the U.K. that has achieved widespread popularity for its unique
   flavor and consistent potency. With origins that stretch back to the
   late 1980s, Cheese is said to descend from a Skunk #1 phenotype whose
   pungent aroma made it stand out. Breeders like Big Buddha Seeds later
   introduced Afghani indica genetics to increase Cheese’s trichome
   production and yields. The resulting hybrid is now well-known for its
   relaxed, happy effects that gently ease you into a blissful state of
   mind.

[file://localhost/product/41/]Afghan "Mazar-i-Sharif" - 20g

   1. All orders need to be payed in bitcoin before we can ship your
   order.
   2. Postal delivery times vary, check our homepage for further
   information.

   your time and it answers most questions.
   Official Product Description:
   Cultivation: Hashish is produced practically everywhere in and around
   Afghanistan. The best kinds of Hash originate from the Northern
   provinces between Hindu Kush and the Russian border (Balkh,
   Mazar-i-Sharif).
   Look
   Very dense, hard and medium brown. It snaps when you bend it far
   enough, but when you get it a little warmer you can easily stick your
   finger nail into it.
   Smell
   Chocolate mint-spice. Typical Afghan with a slightly lighter polm
   scent. When it burns, it smells a little like fine Manali.
   Dutch Magic Description:

White Widow

   [file://localhost/product/1/]

[file://localhost/product/1/]White Widow - 5g

   FREE SHIPPING
   1. All orders need to payed in Bitcoin before we can ship your order.
   2. Postal delivery times vary, check our homepage for further
   information.
   3. We do NOT ship to the U.S.A , Israel or the Netherlands.
   Please check our homepage before mailing us. It's only five minutes of
   your time and it answers most questions.
   Official Product Description:
   Among the most famous strains worldwide is White Widow, a balanced
   hybrid first bred in the Netherlands by Green House Seeds. A cross
   between a Brazilian sativa landrace and a resin-heavy South Indian
   indica, White Widow has blessed every Dutch coffee shop menu since its
   birth in the 1990s. Its buds are white with crystal resin, warning you
   of the potent effects to come. A powerful burst of euphoria and energy
   breaks through immediately, stimulating both conversation and
   creativity. White Widow’s genetics have given rise to many other
   legends like White Russian, White Rhino, and Blue Widow. Still, many
   growers prefer cultivation of the original White Widow, which flowers
   in about 60 days indoors.
   Dutch Magic Description:
   This strain is what harvesters call white widow, its the most common
   sold weed in Holland so it has one of the best price/ratio for
   resellers. It is one of the best selling products we have.
   Thanks for ordering with DutchMagic
   The largest online coffee-shop in the world.

   [file://localhost/product/73/]

[file://localhost/product/73/]Afghan "Mazar-i-Sharif" - 20g

   1. All orders need to be payed in bitcoin before we can ship your

   2. Postal delivery times vary, check our homepage for further
   information.
   3. We do NOT ship to the U.S.A , Israel or the Netherlands.

   your time and it answers most questions.
   Official Product Description:
   Cultivation: Hashish is produced practically everywhere in and around
   Afghanistan. The best kinds of Hash originate from the Northern
   provinces between Hindu Kush and the Russian border (Balkh,
   Mazar-i-Sharif).
   Look
   Very dense, hard and medium brown. It snaps when you bend it far
   enough, but when you get it a little warmer you can easily stick your
   finger nail into it.
   Smell
   Chocolate mint-spice. Typical Afghan with a slightly lighter polm
   scent. When it burns, it smells a little like fine Manali.
   Dutch Magic Description:

[file://localhost/product/76/]White Widow - 10g

   FREE SHIPPING
   1. All orders need to payed in Bitcoin before we can ship your order.

   Official Product Description:
   Among the most famous strains worldwide is White Widow, a balanced
   hybrid first bred in the Netherlands by Green House Seeds. A cross
   between a Brazilian sativa landrace and a resin-heavy South Indian
   indica, White Widow has blessed every Dutch coffee shop menu since its
   birth in the 1990s. Its buds are white with crystal resin, warning you
   of the potent effects to come. A powerful burst of euphoria and energy
   breaks through immediately, stimulating both conversation and
   creativity. White Widow’s genetics have given rise to many other
   legends like White Russian, White Rhino, and Blue Widow. Still, many
   growers prefer cultivation of the original White Widow, which flowers
   in about 60 days indoors.
   Dutch Magic Description:
   This strain is what harvesters call white widow, its the most common

   Dutch Magic Description:
   Very good looking buds! One of our best sellers on past market places
   such as Nucleus and Agora. We receive this from a small harvester who
   takes his time to make his product excellent.
   Official Description:
   Girl Scout Cookies, or GSC, is an OG Kush and Durban Poison hybrid
   cross whose reputation grew too large to stay within the borders of its
   California homeland. With a sweet and earthy aroma, Girl Scout Cookies
   launches you to euphoria’s top floor where full-body relaxation meets a
   time-bending cerebral space. A little goes a long way with this hybrid,
   whose THC heights have won Girl Scout Cookies numerous Cannabis Cup
   awards. Patients needing a strong dose of relief, however, may look to
   GSC for severe pain, nausea, and appetite loss.
   There are several different phenotypes of the Girl Scout Cookies strain
   including Thin Mint and Platinum Cookies, which exhibit some variation
   in appearance and effect. Typically, however, Girl Scout Cookies
   expresses its beauty in twisting green calyxes wrapped in purple leaves
   and fiery orange hairs. Patients and consumers looking to cultivate
   this cannabis staple themselves should wait 9 to 10 weeks for their
   indoor plants to finish flowering.

   Named for its sharply sour aroma, Cheese is an indica-dominant hybrid
   from the U.K. that has achieved widespread popularity for its unique
   flavor and consistent potency. With origins that stretch back to the
   late 1980s, Cheese is said to descend from a Skunk #1 phenotype whose
   pungent aroma made it stand out. Breeders like Big Buddha Seeds later
   introduced Afghani indica genetics to increase Cheese’s trichome
   production and yields. The resulting hybrid is now well-known for its
   relaxed, happy effects that gently ease you into a blissful state of
   mind.

About Us

   WELCOME TO DUTCH MAGIC!
   The largest and longest ongoing online WEED and HASH coffee-shop in the
   world.
   We are here to build up a long-lasting trustworthy relationship with
   all of our customers.
   VERIFY our PGP key (the same since early 2013) via Grams
   http://grams72tru2gdpl2.onion/infodesk/vendor/0x9952ED9F1BAC6AA0
   In early 2013 we started selling our products Silk Road 1, the first
   darknet market place. As most of you know this
   market place was seized by law enforcement. Since then we have been on
   many market places and have seen
   most of them go down one way or another:
   Silk Road 1, Sheep Marketplace, TOR Market, Silk Road 2, Black Market
   Reloaded, Evolution and Nucleus are all examples of this.
   This is why we decided to start our own shop.
   We don't store BTC on our server, all payments are directly from BTC
   wallet to BTC wallet.
   This way your money is safe and no hackers or law enforcement can steal
   your funds.
   We have a very large stock of hash and weed and we are here to give our
   customers the best service possible.
   We have taken a lot of time and effort to make our products here on our
   own shop top dutch coffee shop quality.
   MAIL/MESSAGES:
   If you have a question about an order you placed, please message us in
   the order section.
   Any other questions you can message us directly. Please do not message
   the same thing twice in
   two different message sections.
   We are easy to get along with and here to help should you have any
   questions.
   PGP KEY:
   You may find that we have two keys. However, BOTH are the SAME key.
   Load the key into GPG and see that the KEY ID is,
   and has always been 1BAC6AA0
